24-28 Point Standard Decklists
==============================



 Posted in [PRO TOUR SHADOWS OVER INNISTRAD](/en/events/coverage/ptsoi)
 on April 24, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/generic-avatar-150_9.png)
By By Event Coverage Staff











Twenty-three players earned 24 point or more from their Standard rounds at Pro Tour *Shadows over Innistrad*. Twenty of those players hit exactly 24 points (8-3), two got to 25 points (8-1-1), and just one players received 27 points (9-1).




---

**The following player finished with 27 points (9-1) in Standard:**







#### Lee Shi Tian: Bant Company


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
